 Announces financial assistance of 50-50 thousand rupees and 25-25 thousand rupees for the injured in general

 isse pehle pradhanmantri narendra modi ne aatankwaad se nipatane ke liye nirnaayak karrwai kaa aahvaan kiya or pakistan ko aatankwaad ke poshan kii bhoomi bataaya
 The focus should be on combating sources of terrorism funding such as money laundering, drug trafficking, organized crimes such as criminal activities, decriminalizing terrorist targets as well as misuse of internet including social media by terrorist units
 '' The manifesto stated, "to deal with terrorism successfully, a holistic approach is needed
 aatankwaad ke khilaaf sabhi kadamon main antarrashtriya kanoon barkaraar rakhaa janaa chahie or maanavadhikaron kaa sammaan hona chahie
 '' bricks ne aatankwaad ke khilaaf bahupaksheeya drushtikon ke samanvay main sanyukt raashtra kii kendriya bhoomika par jor dete hue sabhi deshon se aagrah kiya ki ve sanyukt raashtra suraksha parishad ke praasangik prastaavon ko prabhavi tareeke se lagu karen or sanyukt raashtra ke aatankwaad nirodhak ruparekha kii prabhaavashiltaa badhaane ke prati apni patibaddhta doharaayein
 In the manifesto, BRICS stated that it reiterated its commitment to the international standards of the FATF (financial Action Task Force) in combating money laundering and terrorism funding and proliferation
 bricks ne iske saath hi aatankwaad ke vitt poshan se mukaable ke liye efeetief ko jald, prabhavi or saarvbhaumik rup se lagu karne kaa bhi aahvaan kiya
 "we want to increase our cooperation in regional bodies like FATF and FATF," said BRICS
 '' bricks ne apane ghoshnaptr main maadak padaarth ke utpaadan or taskari se utpann vaishvik khatre se nipatane ke liye antarrashtriya or kshetreey sahyog ko majboot karne kaa bhi aahvaan kiya
 He said, "we note with deep concern the growing connection between drug trafficking and terrorism, money laundering and organized crime
" '' usne kaha ki soochna evam sanchaar praudyogiki istemaal main suraksha badhaane main prayaason ko majboot karne kaa ek samjhauta bhi he
 The declaration stated that the group agrees that the emerging challenges for global peace and security and sustainable development generate the need to further enhance its collective efforts
 usne kaha, ''ham is par chintaa jataate hai ki kai deshon main raajnneetik evam suraksha asthirataa dekhne ko mil rahi he jo ki aatankwaad evam atvaad se badhati he
 "we call upon the international community, through the United Nations, the African Union and regional and international partners, to continue our cooperation in addressing these challenges, including post-conflict reconstruction and development efforts," said Bricks
 '' In relation to the tax system, BRICS reiterated its commitment to a globally fair and modern tax system and welcomed the progress made towards the comprehensive implementation of internationally agreed standards
 usne kaha, ''ham bhrashtachar ke saath hi parisampatti vasuuli se jude maamalon or bhrashtachar ke liye vaanchit vyaktiyon ke maamle main antarrashtriya sahyog ko majboot karne kaa samarthan karte hai jisamen bricks bhrashtachar nirodhak kaaryakari samooh ke jariye kiya gaya sahyog bhi shaamil he
 '' ghoshnaptr main kaha gaya, ''ham yah sweekaar karte hai ki avaidh tareeke se arjeet dhanrashi or vittiya pravaah or videshi adhikaar kshetra main rakhi avaidh sampatti sahit bhrashtachar ek vaishvik chunauti he jiskaa aarthik vikaas or satat vikaas par nakaaratmak prabhaav pad saktaa he
 The BRICS also welcomed the Paris Climate Agreement and its expected implementation on November 4

 baad main hamalavar bhi mrit mila
 According to White House press secretary Jay Carney, informing President Barack Obama about the incident, his top national security officials said the incident was not terrorism
 karni ne ek bayaan main kaha, raashtrapati ko bataaya gaya ki visconcin ke brookefield main ek hamalavar tha
 They were told that the firing incident was not linked to terrorism
 obama ko is bare main jaankaree epabiai ke nideshak bob mular, raashtrapati ke chif of staff jaik lu or grih suraksha salaahkaar jon brenan ne di
 He said that the FBI is on the spot and is assisting Brookfield's police department in overcoming the situation
 karni ke mutabik raashtrapati ne epabiai ko nirdesh diya he ki rajya ke tathaa sthaneey adhikariyon ko sangheey sarkaar kaa puraa samarthan milanaa chahie
 The suspect has been identified as 45-year-old Radcliffe F
 Hughton, who was the husband of a spa worker, according to local police and federal investigative agencies
 baad main africa-america redcliff bhi mrit mila

 haalanki usne 36 rafel ladaaku vimaanon ke saude par baatcheet ko aage badhaane ke liye ‘mek in india’ se judi pariyojnaon main bhaag lene kii peshkash kii he
 According to defense sources, the cost will increase if India meets demand on the offset clause, changes in weapons technology and plans to build two hubs for Rafale fighter jets
 ofaset niti sabase pehle san 2005 kii raksha kharid prakriya (dipipi) ke tahat laai gai thi
 Under this, a foreign company has to invest a part of the deal from India here
 raksha sutron ne kaha ki ‘50 pratishat ofaset cloj mul nivida kaa hissaa tha jo 126 ladaaku vimaanon ke liye nikaali gai thi
 Now the French President and Indian Prime Minister have decided to purchase 36 Rafale aircraft directly
 jab france usee dar par vimaanon kii aapurti kii peshkash kar rahaa he jis par vaayu sena kharid rahi he, to 50 pratishat ofaset cloj ke liye kaise kaha ja saktaa he?’ sutron ne kaha ki iske bajaay francisiyon ne ‘mek in india’pahal main shaamil hone kii peshkash kii he

 ’ sutron ne kaha ki francisi sarkaar ne saaf kiya he ki unki companiyaan ‘mek in india’ yojana kaa hissaa bananaa pasand karengi

 francisi keval ofaset cloj ko lekar chintit nahin hai
 The Indian Air Force wants a change in weapons technology so that aircraft can also launch a missile that is not in Rafale
 sutron ke anusaar missile america nirmit he

 in sabase laagat or badhegi
 According to sources, India also wants to set up two centers for 36 Rafale aircraft
 france kii sarkaar ke saath isi tarah ke saude karne vaale katar or misr ne keval ek centre kii maang kii thi
 Sources said, "it is understandable that India's strategic needs may be different but usually two centers are needed when one has more than two squadrons of a particular aircraft
 do kendron kii sthapana par bhi adhik laagat aegi
 During his visit to France, Prime Minister Narendra Modi announced the decision to purchase 36 Rafale fighter jets
 raksha sutron ke anusaar ofaset cloj par, shastr praudyogiki main badlaav par or rafel ladaaku vimaanon ke liye do centre banane kii yojana par bharat kii maang puri karne par laagat main ijapha hoga
